	        	 <div>   
			 				 <P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center; tab-stops: 312.75pt" align=center><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt"><FONT face="Times New Roman">Regulation Governing Capital Adequacy of Commercial Banks<?xml:namespace prefix = o ns = "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:office" /><o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center; tab-stops: 312.75pt" align=center><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center; tab-stops: 312.75pt" align=center><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center; tab-stops: 312.75pt" align=center><B><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Chapter I General Provisions<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 1 Pursuant to the â€œLaw of the Peopleâ€™s Republic of China (PRC) on Banking Regulation and Supervisionâ€, the â€œLaw of the Peopleâ€™s Republic of China on Commercial Banksâ€ and the â€œRegulations of the Peopleâ€™s Republic of China on Foreign Financial Institutionsâ€, this regulation is formulated for the purpose of strengthening the supervision of capital adequacy in commercial banks so as to help commercial banks operate in a safe and sound manner.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 2 This regulation shall be applied to commercial banks incorporated in the PRC, including Chinese-funded commercial banks, solely-foreign-funded commercial banks and Sino-foreign joint-equity commercial banks<U>.</U> </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Article 3 Capital adequacy ratios as referred to in this regulation are the ratios of capitals held by the commercial banks and defined by the regulation to risk-weighted assets of commercial banks.<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt; mso-char-indent-count: -3.75"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Article 4 The calculation and measurement of capital adequacy ratios are on the basis of adequate provisions for various losses, including loan losses.<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Article 5 The amount of capital in commercial banks shall be sufficient enough to cover credit risk and market risk.<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Article 6 Commercial banks shall calculate and measure their capital adequacy on both a stand-alone basis and a consolidated basis. <o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 7 The required minimum ratios shall be no less than 8% for capital adequacy and 4% for core capital adequacy.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 8 The China Banking Regulatory Commission (CBRC) will follow this regulation with respect to reviewing the capital adequacy and capital management of commercial banks.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Article 9 Commercial banks shall disclose capital adequacy information in line with this regulation. <SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN><o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center; tab-stops: 312.75pt" align=center><B><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Chapter II Calculation and Measurement of Capital Adequacy Ratios<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Article 10 In the calculation and measurement of capital adequacy ratios on a consolidated basis, the scope of consolidation shall include the following:<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 63.0pt left 312.75pt; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>Â·</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>financial institutions in which over 50% of the voting shares are owned by commercial banks, which include:<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes"><FONT face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â€</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman">financial institutions in which over 50% of the voting shares are<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>directly owned by the bank;<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â€</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman">financial institutions in which over 50% of the voting shares are indirectly owned by the bank through subsidiaries; and<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â€</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman">financial institutions in which over 50% of the voting shares are directly and indirectly jointly owned by the bank.<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 63.0pt left 312.75pt; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>Â·</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>investments representing less than 50% of the voting shares of <SPAN style="COLOR: black">financial institutions</SPAN>, and meeting one of the following conditions:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â€</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"> the bank owns more than 50% of the voting shares of <SPAN style="COLOR: black">financial institutions</SPAN> through agreements with other investors;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â€</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"> the bank has the power to control the financial and operating policies of <SPAN style="COLOR: black">financial institutions</SPAN> in accordance with articles of association or agreements;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â€</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"> the bank has the power to appoint and remove majority members of boards of directors or other decision making bodies of <SPAN style="COLOR: black">financial institutions</SPAN>; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â€</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"> the bank owns more than 50% of the controlling interest in boards of directors or other decision-making bodies of <SPAN style="COLOR: black">financial institutions</SPAN>;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>The following institutions shall not be included for consolidation:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 63.0pt 99.0pt left 312.75pt; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>Â·</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black">financial institutions</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> that have been closed or declared to be bankrupted;</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 63.0pt 99.0pt left 312.75pt; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>Â·</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black">financial institutions</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> that have been declared to be in liquidation in accordance with the bankruptcy procedures;</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 63.0pt 99.0pt left 312.75pt; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>Â·</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black">financial institutions</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> of which more than 50% of the voting shares are owned as short term investment and will be disposed of within a year; and</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 63.0pt 99.0pt left 312.75pt; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>Â·</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>overseas subsidiaries of <SPAN style="COLOR: black">financial institutions</SPAN> whose movement of capital is controlled by exchange restrictions of host countries or by unexpected events.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 11 The formulae for the capital adequacy ratios are as follows:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 312.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 189pt; TEXT-INDENT: -135pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Capital adequacy ratio = (total capital â€“ deductions) / (risk-weighted assets + 12.5 * capital charge for market risk)</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 189pt; TEXT-INDENT: -135pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 207pt; TEXT-INDENT: -153pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Core capital adequacy ratio = (core capital â€“ deductions) / (risk-weighted assets + 12.5 * capital charge for market risk)</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 0cm"><SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 45.0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>Article 12 The total amount of capital shall consist of core capital and supplementary capital.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 45.0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 48pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 0cm"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>Core capital shall consist of paid-up capital/common stocks, reserves, capital surplus, retained earnings and minority interests.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 48pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 0cm"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 48pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 0cm"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>Supplementary capital shall consist of revaluation reserves, general loan-loss reserves, preference shares, convertible bonds and long-term subordinated debt.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 0cm"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 48pt; TEXT-INDENT: -48pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 0cm"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 13 The amount of supplementary capital shall not exceed 100% of core capital. Long-term subordinated debt in supplementary capital shall not exceed 50% of core capital.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 48pt; TEXT-INDENT: -48pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 0cm"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 14 The following items shall be deducted from the total capital base when calculating the capital adequacy ratio:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">goodwill; </FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">equity investments in the unconsolidated financial institutions; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">equity investments on commercial real estate and equity investments in business enterprises. </FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 48pt; TEXT-INDENT: -48pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 36.0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 15 The following items shall be deducted from the core capital base when calculating the core capital adequacy ratio:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">goodwill;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">50% of the equity investments in the unconsolidated financial institutions; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">50% of equity investments on commercial real estate and 50% of equity investments in business enterprises.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 16 Specific provisions shall be deducted from the book value of loans when commercial banks calculate risk-weighted assets. Other provisions for impairment losses shall also be deducted from the book value of relevant assets items.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 17 Risk weights of foreign claims owned by commercial banks shall be based on the ratings of external credit assessment institutions for the sovereigns or regions. In case there is a discrepancy in ratings for the same sovereign or region, the less favorable rating shall prevail.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">For claims on foreign central governments and central banks, where the rating for the sovereign or region is AA-<SUB> </SUB>or higher, the risk weight is 0%. Otherwise, the risk weight is 100%. </FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">For claims on foreign banks or securities firms, where the rating for the sovereign or region of incorporation is AA- or higher, the risk weight is 20%. Otherwise, the risk weight is 100%.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">For claims on public-sector entities invested<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>by foreign central governments, where the rating for sovereign or region is AA- or higher, the risk weight is 50%. Otherwise, the risk weight is 100%.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 84pt; TEXT-INDENT: -84pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 84pt; TEXT-INDENT: -84pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 18 The risk weight of claims on multilateral development banks is 0%.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 19 The risk weight of claims on the Chinese central government denominated in both domestic and foreign currency is 0%.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>The risk weight of claims on domestic public-sector entities invested by the Chinese central government is 50%.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 20 The risk weight of claims on domestically incorporated policy banks is 0%. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 21 For claims on other domestically incorporated commercial banks with an original maturity of four months or shorter, the risk weight is 0%. Otherwise, the risk weight is 20%.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 22 The risk weight is 0% for claims on specific debts issued by the domestically incorporated financial asset management companies (AMCs) to purchase the state-owned banksâ€™ non-performing loans. The risk weight is 100% for other claims on these AMCs. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 23 The risk weight is 100% for claims on business enterprises, individuals or all other assets. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 24 The risk weight for residential mortgage is 50%. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 71.9pt; TEXT-INDENT: -8.9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 25 The following financial instruments can serve as risk mitigants. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">cash;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">gold;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">bank deposits;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">treasury bonds issued by the Ministry of Finance of the PRC;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman">papers issued by the Peopleâ€™s Bank of China(PBC);<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><A name=OLE_LINK1><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><FONT size=3>Â·</FONT></SPAN></A><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>bonds and papers issued by and bills accepted by policy banks and commercial banks incorporated in the PRC;</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">bonds and papers issued by and bills accepted by the public-sector entities, which are invested by the Chinese central government.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">bonds issued by the central governments, bonds and papers issued by and bills accepted by the central banks, commercial banks and public-sector entities incorporated in countries and regions with AA-<SUP> </SUP>or higher ratings; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">bonds issued by multilateral development banks;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>Loans secured by the above financial instruments shall have the same risk weights as the instruments. In the case of partially secured loans, the secured part gets the correspondingly lower risk weight. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 26 The following guarantors are eligible for risk mitigation:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">policy banks and commercial banks incorporated in the PRC;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">the Chinese government agencies only approved by the State Council, for on-lending of loan proceeds from foreign governments and international financial institutions.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">public-sector entities invested by the Chinese central government.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">central governments, central banks and commercial banks incorporated in countries and regions with AA-<SUP> <SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN></SUP>or higher ratings; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">multilateral development banks;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 44.9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>The risk weights of loans fully guaranteed by the above guarantors shall be the same as those of direct claims on these guarantors. In the case of partially guaranteed loans, the guaranteed portion obtains the lower risk weight accordingly.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>Article 27 Commercial banks shall set aside capital for credit risk for off-balance sheet items. The banks shall calculate risk-weighted assets according to the following steps: </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">converting each off-balance sheet item to credit equivalents by multiplying the nominal principal amounts by a credit conversion factor; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">calculating risk-weighted assets according to the risk weight of<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>the counterparty.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>The current exposure method is used to calculate the risk-weighted assets of foreign exchange contracts, interest rate contracts and other derivative contracts.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black">Article 28<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>Commercial banks shall set aside capital for market risk. </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US>Market risk is defined as the risk of losses in on- and off-balance sheet positions arising from movements in market prices. The risks as referred to in this regulation are:</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 66.05pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12.05pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -.75; mso-para-margin-left: 4.5gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">the risks pertaining to interest rate-related instruments and equities in the trading book; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">foreign exchange risk and commodities risk throughout the bank.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -4.5"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 29 Commercial banks should set up the trading book according to the definition of this regulation. All the items in trading book should be marked to market. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -4.5"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 4.5gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>The trading book includes items as follows: positions in financial instruments that commercial banks take on with the intention of short- term resale or benefiting in the short term from actual or expected differences between the buying and selling prices or from other price or interest rate variations; positions that arise from the execution of trade orders from customers and market making; positions taken in order to hedge other elements of the trading book. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -4.5"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -4.5"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">Article 30 Commercial banks whose trading book positions are more than 10</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"> of the total on- and off-balance sheet assets or more than 8.5 billion RMB are subject to market risk capital charge.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -4.5"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -4.5"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 31 Commercial banks exempted for capital charge for market risk shall report their market risk positions to the CBRC on a quarterly basis. The CBRC will decide on whether banks should be subject to market risk capital charge.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -4.5"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -4.5"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 32 Commercial banks should calculate and measure capital charge for market risk in line with the standardized measurement method in this regulation. Commercial banks can also use internal models to measure market risk subject to the review and approval by the CBRC.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align=center><B><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Chapter III<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>Supervisory Review of Capital Adequacy and Intervention<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 33 The board of directors of each bank shall assume the ultimate responsibility for capital adequacy management. The board has the responsibility for defining the objectives of capital management and risk appetite, and formulating a comprehensive plan to keep capital at an adequate level. In case a board of directors does not exist, the president shall assume the responsibility.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 34 The senior management of commercial banks shall assume the responsibility for the implementation of capital adequacy objectives, which includes stipulating rules on capital adequacy management. With a view to ensuring effective execution of all supervisory measures, the bank shall improve its ability of identifying, measuring and reporting credit risk and market risk, conduct a periodic analysis of the capital adequacy ratios, set up capital management mechanism and strengthen the monitoring of the capital assessment program.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 35 Commercial banks shall report capital adequacy to the CBRC on <SPAN style="COLOR: black">both a stand-alone basis and a consolidated basis</SPAN>. The capital adequacy ratio on a consolidated basis shall be reported semi-annually, and ratio on a stand-alone basis quarterly. In case of material events that affect the capital ratio, the bank shall inform the CBRC in a prompt manner.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Commercial banks shall report to the PBC on capital adequacy while reporting to the CBRC.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -57pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US>Article 36 The CBRC shall review and evaluate banksâ€™ capital adequacy through on-site </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">examination and off-site surveillance, specifically:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">a review of the policies and procedures relating to capital adequacy;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">a review of the comprehensive plan to keep capital at an adequate level and the banksâ€™ capability of monitoring capital adequacy;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">a review of the banksâ€™ credit risk and market risk exposures; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">a review of the banksâ€™ compliance with this regulation in respect of setting the trading book and<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>valuing the trading book items.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>Article 37 The CBRC has the authority to require a higher capital adequacy ratio than the minimum for a particular individual bank in consideration of its risk profile and the capability of risk management.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 38 Commercial banks are classified by the CBRC into three categories on the basis of their capital adequacy status:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">adequately capitalized banks: the capital adequacy ratio is not less than 8%, and the core capital adequacy ratio is not less than 4%; </FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">undercapitalized banks: the capital adequacy ratio is less than 8%, or the core capital adequacy ratio is less than 4%; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">significantly undercapitalized banks: the capital adequacy ratio is less than 4%, or the core capital adequacy ratio is less than 2%.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -57pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US>Article 39 The CBRC encourages adequately capitalized banks to operate in a safe and sound manner</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">. </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US>The CBRC has the authority to intervene at an early stage to prevent bank capital from falling below the minimum levels. The intervention actions may at least include the following:</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -57pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring banks to improve risk management;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring banks to enhance risk controls;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring banks to strengthen the analysis and forecast of capital adequacy; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 57pt; TEXT-INDENT: -12pt"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring banks to submit and implement an acceptable capital maintenance plan, and restricting banks from engaging in high risk activities.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 40 For undercapitalized banks, the CBRC will take the following corrective actions:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">issuing a supervisory letter of notice, which includes a description of the bankâ€™s capital adequacy, </FONT><A name=OLE_LINK2><FONT face="Times New Roman">corrective actions</FONT></A><FONT face="Times New Roman"> to be taken, timeframe for implementation;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring banks to submit and implement an acceptable capital restoration plan within two months after receiving the supervisory letter of notice from the CBRC;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring banks to restrict the asset growth;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring banks to reduce risk assets;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring banks to restrict the purchase of fixed assets;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring banks to restrict dividend<SPAN style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"> payouts or other forms of payment to shareholders</SPAN>; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -.75; mso-para-margin-left: 3.75gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">restricting banks from setting up new branches or starting <SPAN style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">new products and services.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -.75; mso-para-margin-left: 3.75gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>In addition, based on the review of the risk profile and capital restoration of undercapitalized banks, the CBRC has the authority to require the commercial bank to suspend all but low-risk activities, or stop setting up new branches or starting new<SPAN style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"> products and services</SPAN>. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 48pt; TEXT-INDENT: -48pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 48pt; TEXT-INDENT: -48pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US>Article 41 For significantly undercapitalized banks, the CBRC will take further actions in addition to actions listed in Article 40:</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoEndnoteText style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: both; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">requiring removal of senior management; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">taking over the banking institution, facilitating the restructuring of the institution, or <SPAN style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">closing the institution in accordance with relevant laws and regulations</SPAN>.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>For significantly undercapitalized banks, the CBRC shall take into account various external factors and exercise authority to handle the situation with a view to achieving the best results.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align=center><B><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Chapter IV Disclosure<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54.1pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 42 Commercial banksâ€™ boards of directors are responsible for the disclosure of information in respect of capital adequacy. The information to be disclosed must be approved by the board.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45.1pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 43 Commercial banks shall disclose information in respect of capital adequacy periodically. The information shall cover the following five areas:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">objectives and policies of risk management;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">scope of application;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">capital;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">capital adequacy ratios; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">credit risk and market risk.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>In case that the disclosure of certain items of information as required by this regulation may reveal commercial confidential information, banks need not disclose those specific items. But more general information must be disclosed, together with the explanation of why certain specific items have not been disclosed.<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 44 Commercial banks shall disclose the information in respect of capital adequacy within four months after the end of each accounting year. In case the disclosure cannot be made for special factors, the bank shall apply to the CBRC for delay of disclosure at least fifteen days in advance.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 45 Commercial banks shall submit the relevant capital adequacy information to the CBRC prior to disclosure.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 46 Commercial banks shall disclose the information required by this regulation at major operating sites and make sure that the shareholders and relevant stakeholders obtain the information timely.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align=center><B><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Chapter V Supplementary Provisions<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54.1pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Article 47 The calculation, review and information disclosure of capital adequacy ratios in solely-foreign-funded and Sino-foreign joint-equity finance companies shall follow this regulation. The foreign bank domestic branches shall measure risk-weighted assets denominated in RMB in accordance with this regulation.<U><o:p></o:p></U></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt -0.1pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 48 Annex 1, Annex 2, Annex 3, Annex 4 and Annex 5 are integral parts of this regulation, which are as follows:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">Annex 1: Definition of capital</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">Annex 2: Risk weights of on-balance sheet assets</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 117pt; TEXT-INDENT: -63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">Annex 3: Credit conversion factors for off-balance sheet items and definitions</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 117pt; TEXT-INDENT: -63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">Annex 4: The standardized measurement method for market risk capital charge</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 117pt; TEXT-INDENT: -63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">Annex 5: Disclosure<U><o:p></o:p></U></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 2pt 0cm 2pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 49 The notation AA- of Standard &amp; Poolâ€™s is used throughout this regulation, but it does not express the choice of any external credit assessment institution (ECAI) by the CBRC. Commercial banks can choose ECAIs at their discretion, but they should keep consistency in the use of ECAIs over time.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 2pt 0cm 2pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 2pt 0cm 2pt 53.85pt; TEXT-INDENT: -53.85pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 50 Claims on foreign countries or regions include the claims on foreign central governments, central banks and other agencies equivalent to central governments. The definition of agencies equivalent to central governments is based on the definition of relevant home supervisors.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 2pt 0cm 2pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 2pt 0cm 2pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 51 The voting shares as referred to in this regulation are the shares whereby the holder can participate in the company management and have voting rights of making operating decisions.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 2pt 0cm 2pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 1.3pt 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">Article 52 Public sector entities as referred to in this regulation are the operators involved in the provision of public services, which include the supply of water, power, heat, gas, post, communication and transportation services.
