These entities are mainly in the infrastructure sectors of the economy. They are normally set up with government fund, and the size of investment is quite significant.<U><o:p></o:p></U></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 1.3pt 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 1.3pt 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">Article 53<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>Commercial banks shall meet the minimum capital adequacy requirements by 1 January 2007. Banks shall formulate and implement a feasible <SPAN style="COLOR: black">phase-in plan to comply with the requirements</SPAN> during the transition period<SPAN style="COLOR: black">. The CBRC has the authority to take supervisory actions stipulated in Article 40 and 41 in light of the implementation of banksâ€™ capital restoration plans.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45.1pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 54 The power of interpretation of this regulation rests with the CBRC.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -45.1pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt -0.1pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Article 55 This regulation shall come into effect on 1 March 2004.</FONT></SPAN></P><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: å®‹ä½“; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA"><BR style="PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE: always" clear=all></SPAN>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 20pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">Annex 1<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 20pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-line-height-rule: exactly" align=center><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<H1 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: center; tab-stops: 21.0pt; mso-list: none" align=center><B><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><FONT face="Times New Roman">Definition of Capital<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></B></H1>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 30pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 20pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 30pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 20pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>1. Core Capital<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 0.05pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 20pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">Paid-up capital/common stock</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> refers to the capital fully paid by commercial banksâ€™ investors in accordance with the entitiesâ€™ articles of association or agreed terms in the relevant contract and agreement.</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">Capital reserves</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> include share premium, reserves arising from contribution by means of cash or non-cash asset, reserves arising from equity investment, exchange differences arising from the translation of foreign currency capital contribution, differences arising from connected transactions, and other capital reserves.</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">Capital surplus</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> includes statutory surplus reserves, discretionary surplus reserves and statutory public welfare fund.</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">Retained earnings</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> are commercial banksâ€™ retained profit or loss carried forward from previous years.</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.25; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">Minority interests,</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> being minority interests in non-wholly owned subsidiaries on consolidation included in the core capital, refer to the part of net operating results and net assets of subsidiaries which is not directly or indirectly attributable to the parent bank.</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">2. <SPAN style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">S</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">upplementary Capital</SPAN></B><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">Revaluation reserves</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> With the approval of relevant authorities, positive differences between the fair value and the book value of fixed assets arising from the revaluation of commercial banksâ€™ fixed assets are stated as revaluation reserves. These reserves are eligible for inclusion in the supplementary capital if the CBRC considers the revalued amount to be prudent. However, the amount to be included will not exceed 70% of the revaluation reserves.</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3><B><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">General provisions</SPAN></B><SPAN lang=EN-US> are amounts set aside based on a certain percentage of the total amount of outstanding loans. These provisions are used to cover unidentified potential loan losses.</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">Preference shares</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US> are shares issued by commercial banks, which give priority to investors in the appropriation of profit or retained assets.</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman"><B><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Convertible bonds</SPAN></B><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"> are bonds issued by commercial banks in line with relevant legal processes, and could be converted into common stocks in accordance with the agreed terms within a specified period. Convertible bonds could be eligible for inclusion in supplementary capital only if the following conditions are met:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">(1) Bonds are neither secured nor pledged by bank assets, and the right of claim of bondholders is subordinated to that of depositors and other ordinary creditors; and<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">(2) Bonds are not redeemable at the initiative of their holders, or by the issuer without the prior consent of the CBRC. <o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman"><B><SPAN lang=EN-US>Long-term subordinated debt</SPAN></B><SPAN lang=EN-US> is subordinated debt with original fixed terms to maturity of at least five years. With the approval of the CBRC, ordinary long-term subordinated debt of commercial banks, which are neither guaranteed nor secured by bank assets, is eligible for inclusion in the supplementary capital. During the last five years to maturity, the amount to be stated as supplementary capital will be discounted by 20% of the face value each year. For example, a subordinated debt with an initial term of 10 years can be included in the supplementary capital at 100% of its face value in the sixth year, 80% in the seventh year, 60% in the eighth year, 40% in the ninth year and 20% in the last year.</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA"><BR style="PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE: always; mso-special-character: line-break" clear=all></SPAN>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: å®‹ä½“"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>

<P class=MsoEndnoteText style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: both; TEXT-ALIGN: right" align=right><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT face="Times New Roman">100%<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P></TD></TR></TBODY></TABLE>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.6pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">Definitions of off-balance sheet items are as follows:<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -21pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.75; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">1)<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>Direct credit substitutes include general guarantees of indebtedness, forward acceptances and endorsements with character of acceptance.<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 42.0pt; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo12"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>2)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>Certain transaction-related contingent items include bid bonds, performance bonds, prepay bonds and indwelling bonds.<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 42.0pt; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo12"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore">3)<SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN>Short-term trade-related contingencies mainly refer to documentary credits collateralized by underlying shipment with priority to claim.</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 42.0pt; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo12"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore">4)<SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Commitments with original maturity of up to one year, or which can be unconditionally cancelled at any time, include banksâ€™ credit intention agreements.</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 42.0pt; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo12"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore">5)<SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Sale and purchase agreements which credit risks remain with the bank, includes sale and repurchase agreements and asset sales with recourse.</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.6pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">2. Risk assets of exchange rate, interest rate and other derivative contracts<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 14.25pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Exchange rate, interest rate and other derivative contracts mainly refer to the swap, option, future and precious metals trading. </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">The amount of risk asset of these contracts can be calculated by the current exposure method. The risk asset of interest rate and foreign exchange rate contract is the sum of the replacement cost obtained by marking to market and an amount calculated on the basis of the total notional principal amount of its book value multiplied by different factors. Factors can be split by the residual maturity as follows:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>

<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; tab-stops: list 36.0pt; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo14"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><B><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>I.</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></B><B><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>Interest rate risk<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></B></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Interest rate risk covers risk of debt securities (both fixed-rate and floating-rate debt securities and instruments, negotiable certificates of deposit, non-convertible preference shares, and also convertible bonds which trade like debt securities), interest rate derivatives and debt securities derivatives in the trading book. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>The capital charge for interest rate risk consists of two parts: one is for specific risk and the other is for general market risk: </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 39.0pt; mso-list: l2 level2 lfo14"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>1.</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>Specific risk </FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Specific risk charge is graduated in five broad categories as follows:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.5"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">government<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>0.00</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes"><FONT face="Times New Roman">&nbsp; </FONT></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.5"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>qualifying <U><o:p></o:p></U></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 153pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; tab-stops: 189.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: -3.0; mso-para-margin-left: 9.75gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">0.25</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">(residual term to final maturity 6 months or less)</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -7.7pt 0pt 153pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; tab-stops: 189.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: -3.0; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -.64gd; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: 9.75gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">1.00</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">(residual term to final maturity between 6 and 24 months)</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 153pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; tab-stops: 189.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: -3.0; mso-para-margin-left: 9.75gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">1.60</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">(residual term to final maturity exceeding 24 months)</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 33.6pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.8"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>other<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>8.00</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 33.6pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.8"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 39.0pt; mso-list: l2 level2 lfo14"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>2.</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>General market risk </FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45.5pt; mso-para-margin-left: 3.79gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>The capital charge for general market risk consists of three parts as follows:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45.5pt; mso-para-margin-left: 3.79gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 60.75pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: 45.0pt list 60.75pt left 63.0pt 126.0pt 189.0pt; mso-list: l14 level2 lfo13"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>(1)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'"> </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>The vertical capital charge for the matched portion of weighted long and short positions in each time-band;</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 60.75pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 60.75pt; mso-list: l14 level2 lfo13"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(2)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>The horizontal capital charge for the matched portion of weighted long and short positions across different time-bands; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 60.75pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 60.75pt; mso-list: l14 level2 lfo13"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(3)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>The capital charge for weighted net long or short positions (absolute value) in the trading book.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 44.9pt; mso-para-margin-left: 3.74gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>The maturity method is applied to the calculation of capital charge for general market risk. Time-bands and weights are set out in Table 1. Time-zones and weights are set out in the Table 2.<B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><o:p></o:p></B></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 44.9pt; mso-para-margin-left: 3.74gd"><B><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; mso-para-margin-left: 3.75gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>The maturity method for calculating the capital charge for general market risk is as follows:<B><o:p></o:p></B></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 69pt; TEXT-INDENT: -24pt; mso-char-indent-count: -2.0; mso-para-margin-left: 3.75gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“">(1)</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"> Multiply the positions reported in each time-band by a risk factor shown in the Table 1;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 69pt; TEXT-INDENT: -24pt; mso-char-indent-count: -2.0; mso-para-margin-left: 3.75gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“">(2) </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">Multiply the matched portion of the weighted long and short positions in each time-band by 10</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"> to get the vertical capital charge;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 3.75gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“">(3</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">) Offset the weighted long and short positions in each time-band, resulting in weighted net positions of each time-band; in each time-zone multiply the matched portion of all time-bandsâ€™ weighted net positions by the first column of factors in the Table 2 to get the horizontal capital charge in each time-zone;</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 3.75gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“">(4) </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">Offset the weighted net positions of all time-bonds in each time-zone, resulting in weighted net positions of each time-zone; multiply the matched portion of every two time-zonesâ€™ weighted net positions by the second column of factor in the Table 2 to get the horizontal capital charge across different time-zones; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 62.9pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: 63.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 3.74gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">(5) Offset t</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“">he </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">weighted net positions of all time-zones to get the weighted net long or short positions in the whole trading book.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>

<P class=MsoCaption style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal"><B><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">Table 2: time-zones and weights<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><B><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>3. Interest rate and debt bond derivatives</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 40.3pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Interest rate derivatives include derivatives contracts and off-balance sheet instruments which react to changes in interest rates, e.g. interest rate futures, forward rate agreements (FRAs), interest rate and cross currency swaps, interest rate options and forward foreign exchange positions. Debt derivatives include bond futures and bond options.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 40.3pt"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 40.3pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Derivatives mentioned above should be first converted into positions in the relevant underlying and become subject to specific risk and general market risk charges as described above. Interest rate and cross currency swaps, FRAs, forward foreign exchange contracts and interest rate futures will not be subject to a specific risk charge. In the case of futures contracts where the underlying instrument is a debt security, or an index representing a basket of debt securities, a specific risk charge will be required according to the credit risk of the issuer. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 40.3pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; tab-stops: list 36.0pt; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo14"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>II.</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>Equity risk </FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Equity risk refers to the risk related to positions of equity and equity derivatives in the trading book. Equity is defined as all instruments that exhibit market behavior similar to equities<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>including common stocks (whether voting or non-voting), convertible securities that behave like equities and commitments to buy or sell equities. </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39.75pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 39.75pt; mso-list: l9 level1 lfo5"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore">1ï¼Ž</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US>Specific risk and general market risk</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21.75pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39.75pt"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">The capital charge for specific risk is the sum of various marketsâ€™ values, each of which equals to the value of multiplying the sum of the absolute value of the net positions of all equities in each market by 8</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">.The capital charge for general market risk is the sum of the values, each of which equals to the value of multiplying the absolute value of the net matched position after offsetting of all equities in each market by 8</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39.75pt"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">2</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“">.</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">Equity derivatives</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 35.9pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0.1pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 35.9pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0.1pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Equity derivatives include forwards, futures and swaps on both individual equities and stock indices.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 35.9pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0.1pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 35.9pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0.1pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>The derivatives should be converted into positions in the relevant underlying and become subject to specific risk and general market risk charges as described above.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 35.9pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0.1pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; tab-stops: list 36.0pt left 45.0pt; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo14"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>III.</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>Foreign exchange risk</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 35.9pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Foreign exchange risk refers to the risk related to the positions of foreign exchange (including gold) and foreign exchange derivatives.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 35.9pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: 0cm list 39.0pt; mso-list: l2 level2 lfo14"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>1.</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>The capital charge for foreign exchange risk equals to the value of multiplying the overall net open position by 8</FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; tab-stops: 0cm"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN-LEFT: 35.9pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song"><FONT size=3>The overall net open position equals to the sum of two items as follows:<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="MARGIN-LEFT: 35.9pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 3.0gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">(1) the sum of the net long positions or the sum of the net short positions (absolute value)<B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"> </B>of the<B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"> </B>portfolio of foreign currency (gold is not included), whichever is the greater;<B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN></B><SPAN style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">and</SPAN><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><o:p></o:p></B></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 3.0gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>(2) the net position in gold.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 3.0gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 39pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 39.0pt; mso-list: l2 level2 lfo14"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>2.</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>Foreign exchange derivatives</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 35.9pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>The derivatives should be converted into positions in the relevant underlying and become subject to specific risk and general market risk charges as described above.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 35.9pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.99gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 6pt; mso-char-indent-count: .5"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>IV. Commodities risk </FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Commodities risk refers to the risk related to the positions of commodities, commodity forwards, commodity futures and commodity swaps.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 1.45pt; mso-char-indent-count: .12; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Commodities as referred to in this regulation are physical products which are or can be traded on a secondary market, e.g. precious metals (gold is not included), agricultural products and minerals (including oil).</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 1.45pt; mso-char-indent-count: .12; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>The capital charge for commodities risk should be the sum of two items as follows:</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; TEXT-INDENT: -15pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.25; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">(1) the result of multiplying the sum of<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>the absolute value of the net position of each category of commodities by 15</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">; and</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; TEXT-INDENT: -15pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.25; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">(2) the result of multiplying the sum of<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>the gross position of each category of commodities (long positions plus absolute values of short positions) by 3</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">â„…</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; TEXT-INDENT: -15pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.25; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 27pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.25gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>Commodity derivatives should be converted into notional commodities positions, and become subject to the commodity risk charge as described above.</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 48pt; mso-para-margin-left: 4.0gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 6pt; mso-char-indent-count: .5"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>V. Options risk</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 48.85pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: list 48.85pt; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo15"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>1.</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3>Banks that solely use purchased options will be free to use the simplified approach.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 30.85pt"><U><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><SPAN style="TEXT-DECORATION: none"><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></SPAN></o:p></SPAN></U></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45.05pt; TEXT-INDENT: -14.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.17; mso-para-margin-left: 2.58gd"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman"><B><SPAN lang=EN-US>(1)</SPAN></B><SPAN lang=EN-US> The capital charge for long cash and long put or short cash and long call will be the market value of the underlying of the option multiplied by the sum of specific and general market risk charges for the underlying less the amount the option in the money (if any), with the reduced capital charge bounded at zero.<B><o:p></o:p></B></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45.05pt; TEXT-INDENT: -14.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.17; mso-para-margin-left: 2.58gd"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman"><B><SPAN lang=EN-US>(2)</SPAN></B><SPAN lang=EN-US> The capital charge will be the lesser of the market value of the underlying of the option multiplied by the sum of specific and general market risk charges for the underlying and the market value of the option.</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -14.05pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.17; mso-para-margin-left: 2.58gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">(3) The capital charge for special risk and general market risk of the underlying instruments should be calculated according to the following table:<B><o:p></o:p></B></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 41.05pt; mso-para-margin-left: 3.42gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>

<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: margin; mso-element-left: right; mso-element-top: 15.6pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>6 months or less</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: margin; mso-element-left: right; mso-element-top: 15.6pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>Over 6 months to 24 months</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: margin; mso-element-left: right; mso-element-top: 15.6pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>Over 24 months</FONT></SPAN></P>

<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -32.05pt; mso-char-indent-count: -2.67; mso-para-margin-left: 2.58gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -32.05pt; mso-char-indent-count: -2.67; mso-para-margin-left: 2.58gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>commodity,</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: -32.05pt; mso-char-indent-count: -2.67; mso-para-margin-left: 2.58gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">VU </FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“">=</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"> the market value of the underlying instrumen</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“">tÃ—15%</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman">.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 30.85pt; tab-stops: 18.0pt 45.0pt 54.0pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.57gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 30.85pt; tab-stops: 18.0pt 45.0pt 54.0pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.57gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>Add gamma impacts of all options on the same underlying instrument together to get the net gamma impact of the underlying instrument. Add the absolute values of these net gamma impacts together to get the total capital charge for gamma risk if the net gamma impact of the underlying instrument is minus.<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 30.85pt; tab-stops: 18.0pt 45.0pt 54.0pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.57gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 30.85pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt 54.0pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.57gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>(3) C<SPAN style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">apital charge for Vega risk<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 30.85pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt 54.0pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.57gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 30.85pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt 54.0pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.57gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>capital charge for vega risk of a underlying instrument<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 120.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt 54.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 8.56gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"><FONT face="Times New Roman">=</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">â”‚</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"><FONT face="Times New Roman">(25% - the volatility of the underlying instrument * the sum of the Vegas for all options on the underlying instrument</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">â”‚<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 120.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt 54.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 8.56gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 30.85pt; tab-stops: 45.0pt 54.0pt; mso-para-margin-left: 2.57gd"><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman">The total capital charge for Vega risk equals the sum of the capital charges for Vega risk of all <SPAN style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">underlying instruments.</SPAN><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><o:p></o:p></B></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA"><BR style="PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE: always" clear=all></SPAN>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold"><FONT size=3><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN>Annex 5<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>

<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 40.05pt; TEXT-INDENT: -16.05pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -1.0; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">Events which may cause capital base increasing/decreasing or organization separating/consolidating in reporting period.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN-LEFT: 24pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: å®‹ä½“; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face="å®‹ä½“, MS Song">Significant equity investment events in reporting period.</FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; tab-stops: 63.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<H2 style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-style: italic"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>4. Capital adequacy ratios<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></H2>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-style: italic"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>The bank should explain the capital strategy and capital adequacy assessing approach, and disclose the factors relevant to capital adequacy. The following items should be disclosed in details:<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-style: italic"><FONT face="Times New Roman">The total amount of risk-weighted assets of on-balance sheet<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-style: italic"><FONT face="Times New Roman">The total amount of risk-weighted assets of off-balance sheet<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-style: italic"><FONT face="Times New Roman">The total amount of risk-weighted assets<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT face="Times New Roman">Capital charge for market risk<SPAN style="mso-bidi-font-style: italic"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Â·</SPAN><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-style: italic">Capital adequacy ratio and core capital adequacy ratio on </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="COLOR: black">a stand-alone basis</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-style: italic"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-style: italic"><FONT face="Times New Roman">Capital adequacy ratio and core capital adequacy ratio on a consolidated basis<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto"><o:p><FONT face="Times New Roman" size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><FONT size=3>5. Credit risk and market risk<o:p></o:p></FONT></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 9pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT face="Times New Roman">Credit risk <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -2.85pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: .75gd; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo10"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(1)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>strategies of credit risk management and controlling<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -2.85pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: .75gd; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo10"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(2)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>organizational structure and responsibility of credit risk management<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -2.85pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: .75gd; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo10"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(3)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>names of ECAIs used to calculate risk weights, plus reason for changes<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -2.85pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: .75gd; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo10"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(4)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>the amount of credit risk exposure<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -2.85pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: .75gd; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo10"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(5)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>the opening and closing balance of non-performance loan<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -2.85pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: .75gd; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo10"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(6)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>provisioning and reporting approach of general provision, special provision and specific provision<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -2.85pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: .75gd; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo10"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(7)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>the opening and closing balance of general<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>provision, special provision and specific provision; the respective amount of provisions setting aside, recovering and writing-off in reporting period<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -2.85pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: .75gd; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo10"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(8)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>the main principle to identify qualifying collaterals, the ratio of the collateral value to the principal of loans which is internally decided<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; tab-stops: list 27.0pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-char-indent-count: -1.5; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: -2.85pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-para-margin-left: .75gd; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo10"><FONT face="Times New Roman"><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><SPAN style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT size=3>(9)</FONT><SPAN style="FONT: 7pt 'Times New Roman'">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT size=3>the relevant management principle of guarantee loan.<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm -2.85pt 0pt 9pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312">Â·</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-fareast-font-family: ä»¿å®‹_GB2312"><FONT face="Times New Roman">Market risk <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
